msg:Aijing International Hotel in Wenchang 
2024/02/06-08
Front desk not really helpful. Just want you to go as it was the whole time "OK, OK..." and "I'll take you to your room"...
But no help with luggage, nor an answer if the kitchen would have something for me to eat... I sent my list of allergies (gluten, dairy, egg, honey and soy) to the hotel's wechat the evening so that they could give it to the kitchen...
First room:
The fridge was not cold.
Bathroom floor wet and entrance floor dirty ğŸ˜°

The manager came and was friendly and helpful. He helped me with my luggage to another room 8505, which was larger.
Here the fridge was also not really making cold and switched off when going out. They couldn't give an extra card for electricity.

In the morning the manager showed me the different food at the buffet that I could eat, but I never received the pork etc, he promised the previous evening, for breakfast nor answered my message when I asked if I should wait for it...
For breakfast I could eat the fruit and in a steam basket a piece of corn-on-the-cob, sweet potato, yam and taro. They also had corn flakes.
Interesting they had 3 milk options: cow milk, soy milk and coconut milk...
The second evening I spent an hour on Wechat with reception to find out if the kitchen could prepare something for me with my allergies - I did give it the previous evening.... Then I went for a walk on the beach... When I came back, they hadn't prepared the fish! The manager gave me a coconut with a straw to drink the juice...
So I only wasted my time to find out if they could prepare something - I did give them my list in Chinese of what I cannot eat...ğŸ˜° Luckily I always have some food with me...

The fish tanks are outside the dining room so you can choose your fish fresh.... As in most places in China ğŸ˜Š

Swimming pool was empty.

Good comfortable beds.
Down duvets.
Nice spacious room with little balcony, but balcony has a concrete wall, not glass to see through...
From the premises you go directly onto the beach!
Very nice quiet environment away from the crowds! After the fireworks at 21:00 the outside lights were switched off and then you only hear the sea...

If you do not have transport, it is a bit far, but if you want to go and rest for a few days, away from crowds, then this is a good place ğŸ˜ğŸ¤ ğŸŒ»ğŸï¸ğŸ–ï¸
Thete are charging facilities for electric cars...

ğŸ¨Hotel guide:
Detailed address: Located at No. 10 Yeyuan Road, Dongjiao Coconut Grove Scenic Area, Dongjiao Town, Wenchang City, Wenchang Dongjiao Coconut Grove Melon International Hotel

Hotel features:
270-degree panoramic floor-to-ceiling glass provides an unrivaled view of the landscape. It focuses on leisure and comfort, luxury and restraint, simplicity and extraordinary. When taking a bubble bath at night, pull up the curtains and take photos in seconds. Stand on the balcony and look down at the sea, sunshine, and beach. , panoramic view, great experience.

Must experience:
